  contents: # 知己项目 · 本地模型 + Auto 推荐开发模式

> 结合 qwen2.5 本地模型与 task_router 自动推荐，低成本、高效率开发

---

## 一、核心理念

```
简单步骤 → qwen2.5（本地，零API成本）
复杂步骤 → Claude（高级，保证质量）
```

**目标**：拆解后按步分配模型，组合回答，省 Token、省费用。

---

## 二、开发流程

```
用户需求
    │
    ▼
1️⃣ 理解+拆解（本地模型）
    │  decompose_to_plan() → 本地 qwen2.5 做 analyze_task
    │
    ▼
2️⃣ 每步 auto 推荐模型
    │  task_router.auto_route() / decompose 返回的 recommended_model
    │
    ▼
3️⃣ 按步执行
    │  简单：ollama run qwen2.5:1.5b
    │  复杂：Cursor 高级模型
    │
    ▼
4️⃣ 组合输出
```

---

## 三、调用方式

### 3.1 任务拆解（本地模型）

```python
# 卡若AI 根目录下执行
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, "/Users/karuo/Documents/个人/卡若AI")

from _共享模块.task_decomposer import decompose_to_plan

plan = decompose_to_plan("知己网站MVP：首页、产品介绍、合作入口")
# plan["steps"] 每步含 recommended_model
```

### 3.2 单步模型推荐

```python
from _共享模块.task_router import auto_route, should_use_local_model

# 一键路由
r = auto_route("帮我拆解知己网站的需求")
# r["use_local"], r["model"], r["command"]

# 仅判断
use_local, model = should_use_local_model("生成Next.js首页代码")
```

### 3.3 本地模型直接调用

```bash
# 摘要、拆解、简单问答
echo "知己项目三条主线是什么？" | ollama run qwen2.5:1.5b
```

```python
from _共享模块.local_llm import summarize, analyze_task, classify

# 摘要
summarize("1.19流光对话内容...")

# 任务分析
analyze_task("知己网站MVP需要哪些页面？")
```

> 基于 1.19 流光对话整理 | 本地模型+auto推荐模式开发

## 1. 项目背景

### 1.1 项目名称
**知己（ZhiJi）** — 人与关系成长平台

### 1.2 三条主线（流光 1.19 对话）

| 主线 | 内容 | 优先级 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **软件** | 核心竞争力，最小成本先开发 MVP | P0 |
| **产品体系** | 线上训练营、一对一咨询、线下沙龙 | P0 |
| **老师资源** | 原型领导力、MBTI、荣格12原型等 | P0 |

### 1.3 目标市场

| 市场 | 产品力 | 合作方 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 高校 | 职业力、职业规划 | 上海 INFP 77年、高校资源 |
| 家庭/婚恋 | 幸福力、情感力、情绪力 | 妍希、乐萌 |
| 职场/企业 | 原型领导力、团队高绩效 | 上海原型领导力 Sandy/张磊 |
| 流量端 | 引流、内容策划 | 玉爷、阿明 |

---

## 2. 网站 MVP 范围（金水木火土）

### 2.1 金 - 定标架构
- 品牌一句话定位
- 团队/老师展示
- 核心价值主张

### 2.2 水 - 流程规划
- 产品/课程介绍
- 预约/咨询入口
- 合作流程说明

### 2.3 木 - 落地推进
- 产品矩阵（训练营、咨询、沙龙）
- 价格/权益展示
- 合作案例

### 2.4 火 - 运营迭代
- 学员反馈
- 数据/成果展示

### 2.5 土 - 投资裂变
- 合作/招商入口
- 联系方式
- 资源对接

---

## 3. 技术需求（简要）

- **前端**：Next.js 14+ / Shadcn UI / Tailwind / TypeScript
- **部署**：Vercel 或宝塔
- **开发模式**：本地模型+auto推荐（见 `本地模型auto推荐开发模式.md`）

---

## 4. 开发流程

```
1. 理解+拆解（本地 qwen2.5）→ decompose_to_plan
2. 每步 auto 推荐模型 → task_router.auto_route
3. 简单步骤 → ollama qwen2.5
4. 复杂步骤（架构/代码）→ Claude
5. 组合输出
```

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/知己/web/components/MobileBottomNav.tsx
  contents: "use client"

import Link from "next/link"
import { usePathname } from "next/navigation"
import { Home, BookOpen, Handshake, Mail } from "lucide-react"

const items = [
  { href: "/", label: "首页", icon: Home },
  { href: "/products", label: "产品", icon: BookOpen },
  { href: "/cooperation", label: "合作", icon: Handshake },
  { href: "/contact", label: "联系", icon: Mail },
]

export function MobileBottomNav() {
  const pathname = usePathname()
  return (
    <nav className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-50 border-t bg-white/90 backdrop-blur safe-area-inset-bottom md:hidden">
      <div className="flex justify-around h-16">
        {items.map(({ href, label, icon: Icon }) => {
          const active = pathname === href
          return (
            <Link
              key={href}
              href={href}
              className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center flex-1 min-h-[44px] min-w-[44px] text-xs active:bg-orange-50 transition-colors"
            >
              <Icon className={`w-5 h-5 mb-0.5 ${active ? "text-orange-500" : "text-muted-foreground"}`} />
              <span className={active ? "text-orange-600 font-medium" : "text-muted-foreground"}>{label}</span>
            </Link>
          )
        })}
      </div>
    </nav>
  )
}

## 二、2026年1月关键进展

### 2.1 团队组建
- **大大**：职业经理人，ETJ，半年 5 万，牵头推进、运营 2 号位
- **阿明**：深圳→杭州，执行力靠前，活动组织、与合作方对接
- **妍希、乐萌**：线下疗愈师、沙龙产品
- **冰（玉斌）**：待定，作为流光团队侧合作，小俊/美玲对接卡若

### 2.2 上海原型领导力
- **Sandy 老师**：INTJ，荣格 12 原型、企业领导力培训
- **张磊老师**：INFP，企业高管教练，《企业数字化转型》
- **合作点**：理论体系成熟、企业资源、数字中台、企业家圈子
- **高校 INFP 77 年**：职业力、产品体系设计，可做合伙人

### 2.3 玉爷合作
- **模式**：玉爷做流量、流光组织导师资源
- **定位**：咨询师/包工头，玉爷引流、流光组织人
- **产品**：线上训练营、MBTI 体系

### 2.4 线下沙龙
- **妍希**：Panda 孵化、线下沙龙内测
- **乐萌**：疗愈师、活动交付
- **阿明**：生态有数圈子、组活动经验

### 2.5 公司主体
- **沐风无界教育科技有限公司**：阿猫可变更，无负债
- **成立节奏**：4 月失业金领完、核心骨干到位后

You have access to MCP (Model Context Protocol) tools through the MCP FileSystem.

## MCP Tool Access

You have a `call_mcp_tool` tool available that allows you to call any MCP tool from the enabled MCP servers. To use MCP tools effectively:

1. **Discover Available Tools**: Browse the MCP tool descriptors in the file system to understand what tools are available. Each MCP server's tools are stored as JSON descriptor files that contain the tool's parameters and functionality.

2. **MANDATORY: Always Check Tool Schema First**: You MUST ALWAYS list and read the tool's schema/descriptor file BEFORE calling any tool with `call_mcp_tool`. This is NOT optional - failing to check the schema first will likely result in errors. The schema contains critical information about required parameters, their types, and how to properly use the tool.

The MCP tool descriptors live in the /Users/karuo/.cursor/projects/Users-karuo-Documents-AI/mcps folder. Each enabled MCP server has its own folder containing JSON descriptor files (for example, /Users/karuo/.cursor/projects/Users-karuo-Documents-AI/mcps/<server>/tools/tool-name.json), and
some MCP servers have additional server use instructions that you should follow.

## MCP Resource Access

You also have access to MCP resources through the `list_mcp_resources` and `fetch_mcp_resource` tools. MCP resources are read-only data provided by MCP servers. To discover and access resources:

1. **Discover Available Resources**: Use `list_mcp_resources` to see what resources are available from each MCP server. Alternatively, you can browse the resource descriptor files in the file system at /Users/karuo/.cursor/projects/Users-karuo-Documents-AI/mcps/<server>/resources/resource-name.json.

2. **Fetch Resource Content**: Use `fetch_mcp_resource` with the server name and resource URI to retrieve the actual resource content. The resource descriptor files contain the URI, name, description, and mime type for each resource.

Available MCP servers:

<mcp_file_system_server name="cursor-ide-browser" folderPath="/Users/karuo/.cursor/projects/Users-karuo-Documents-AI/mcps/cursor-ide-browser" serverUseInstructions="The cursor-ide-browser is an MCP server that allows you to navigate the web and interact with the page. Use this for frontend/webapp development and testing code changes.

CRITICAL - Lock/unlock workflow:
1. browser_lock requires an existing browser tab - you CANNOT lock before browser_navigate
2. Correct order: browser_navigate -> browser_lock -> (interactions) -> browser_unlock
3. If a browser tab already exists (check with browser_tabs list), call browser_lock FIRST before any interactions
4. Only call browser_unlock when completely done with ALL browser operations for this turn

IMPORTANT - Before interacting with any page:
1. Use browser_tabs with action "list" to see open tabs and their URLs
2. Use browser_snapshot to get the page structure and element refs before any interaction (click, type, hover, etc.)

IMPORTANT - Waiting strategy:
When waiting for page changes (navigation, content loading, animations, etc.), prefer short incremental waits (1-3 seconds) with browser_snapshot checks in between rather than a single long wait. For example, instead of waiting 10 seconds, do: wait 2s -> snapshot -> check if ready -> if not, wait 2s more -> snapshot again. This allows you to proceed as soon as the page is ready rather than always waiting the maximum time.

Notes:
- Native dialogs (alert/confirm/prompt) never block automation. By default, confirm() returns true and prompt() returns the default value. To test different responses, call browser_handle_dialog BEFORE the triggering action: use accept: false for "Cancel", or promptText: "value" for custom prompt input.
- Iframe content is not accessible - only elements outside iframes can be interacted with.
- Use browser_type to append text, browser_fill to clear and replace. browser_fill also works on contenteditable elements.
- For nested scroll containers, use browser_scroll with scrollIntoView: true before clicking elements that may be obscured." />

import Link from "next/link"
import { useSearchParams } from "next/navigation"
import { useState, Suspense } from "react"
import { Mail, ArrowLeft, Phone, MessageCircle, Send } from "lucide-react"

const PRODUCT_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  online: "线上训练营",
  consult: "一对一高客单咨询",
  salon: "线下沙龙",
}

const TYPE_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  enterprise: "企业合作",
  mentor: "导师/资源对接",
}

const MARKET_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  gaoxiao: "高校职业力",
  jiating: "家庭幸福力",
  zhichang: "职场领导力",
  liuliang: "流量/内容",
}

function ContactContent() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams()
  const product = searchParams.get("product")
  const type = searchParams.get("type")
  const market = searchParams.get("market")

  const [name, setName] = useState("")
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("")
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState("")
  const [message, setMessage] = useState("")

  const contextParts: string[] = []
  if (product) contextParts.push(`产品：${PRODUCT_LABELS[product] || product}`)
  if (type) contextParts.push(`类型：${TYPE_LABELS[type] || type}`)
  if (market) contextParts.push(`市场：${MARKET_LABELS[market] || market}`)
  const contextStr = contextParts.length > 0 ? contextParts.join(" | ") : ""

  const emailSubject = contextStr
    ? `【知己】咨询：${contextStr}`
    : "【知己】合作咨询"

  const emailBody = [
    "您好，",
    "",
    ...(contextStr ? [`咨询意向：${contextStr}`, ""] : []),
    "--- 请填写以下信息 ---",
    `姓名：${name || "（请填写）"}`,
    `邮箱：${email || "（请填写）"}`,
    `电话：${phone || "（请填写）"}`,
    "",
    "留言：",
    message || "（请填写您的需求或问题）",
  ].join("\n")

  const mailtoHref = `mailto:contact@zhiji.example.com?subject=${encodeURIComponent(emailSubject)}&body=${encodeURIComponent(emailBody)}`

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    window.location.href = mailtoHref
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50">
      <div className="py-8 md:py-12 px-4">
        <div className="mx-auto max-w-5xl">
          <Link
            href="/"
            className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground mb-6 min-h-[44px]"
          >
            <ArrowLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
            返回首页
          </Link>
          <h1 className="text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold mb-2">联系我们</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-6">合作洽谈、产品咨询、资源对接、预约咨询</p>

          {contextStr && (
            <div className="mb-8 p-4 rounded-xl bg-orange-50 border border-orange-100">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-orange-700">
                您正在咨询：{contextStr}
              </p>
            </div>
          )}

          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4 mb-10">
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="name" className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1.5">
                姓名
              </label>
              <input
                id="name"
                type="text"
                value={name}
                onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请输入您的姓名"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border bg-white focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-200 focus:border-orange-300 outline-none transition min-h-[44px]"
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="email" className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1.5">
                邮箱
              </label>
              <input
                id="email"
                type="email"
                value={email}
                onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请输入您的邮箱"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border bg-white focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-200 focus:border-orange-300 outline-none transition min-h-[44px]"
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="phone" className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1.5">
                电话
              </label>
              <input
                id="phone"
                type="tel"
                value={phone}
                onChange={(e) => setPhone(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请输入您的电话"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border bg-white focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-200 focus:border-orange-300 outline-none transition min-h-[44px]"
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="message" className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1.5">
                留言
              </label>
              <textarea
                id="message"
                value={message}
                onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请描述您的需求或问题..."
                rows={4}
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border bg-white focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-200 focus:border-orange-300 outline-none transition resize-none"
              />
            </div>
            <button
              type="submit"
              className="w-full inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 px-6 py-3.5 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-amber-500 text-white font-medium hover:opacity-90 transition-opacity min-h-[48px]"
            >
              <Send className="w-4 h-4" />
              发送邮件
            </button>
          </form>

          <div className="space-y-4 mb-10">
            <a
              href={mailtoHref}
              className="flex items-center justify-between p-5 rounded-2xl border bg-white shadow-sm hover:shadow-md hover:border-orange-200 transition-all active:scale-[0.99] min-h-[72px]"
            >
              <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                  <Mail className="w-6 h-6 text-orange-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h2 className="font-semibold">直接发邮件</h2>
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">contact@zhiji.example.com</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </a>
            <a
              href="tel:4000000000"
              className="flex items-center justify-between p-5 rounded-2xl border bg-white shadow-sm hover:shadow-md hover:border-orange-200 transition-all active:scale-[0.99] min-h-[72px]"
            >
              <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-amber-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                  <Phone className="w-6 h-6 text-amber-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h2 className="font-semibold">拨打电话</h2>
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">400-000-0000</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </a>
            <a
              href="https://www.feishu.cn"
              target="_blank"
              rel="noopener noreferrer"
              className="flex items-center justify-between p-5 rounded-2xl border bg-white shadow-sm hover:shadow-md hover:border-orange-200 transition-all active:scale-[0.99] min-h-[72px]"
            >
              <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-yellow-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                  <MessageCircle className="w-6 h-6 text-yellow-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h2 className="font-semibold">飞书沟通</h2>
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">添加飞书好友</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </a>
          </div>

          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3">
            <Link
              href="/products"
              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-3.5 rounded-xl border-2 border-orange-200 text-orange-600 font-medium hover:bg-orange-50 transition-colors min-h-[44px]"
            >
              查看产品
            </Link>
            <Link
              href="/cooperation"
              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-3.5 rounded-xl border-2 border-orange-200 text-orange-600 font-medium hover:bg-orange-50 transition-colors min-h-[44px]"
            >
              合作入口
            </Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

export default function ContactPage() {
  return (

assistant:
<think>
The layout looks fine. focus:not-sr-only might need to be focus:fixed or the Tailwind class - actually sr-only makes it hidden, and on focus we want it to show. In Tailwind, focus:not-sr-only might not work - sr-only applies many utility classes. Let me use focus:fixed focus:block or similar. Actually the standard pattern is:
- sr-only: hides the element
- focus: block it and position it on focus

In Tailwind v4 or v3, we'd need something like:
```
className="sr-only focus:not-sr-only focus:absolute ..."
```

Actually `not-sr-only` is not a Tailwind class. The pattern for skip link is:
- By default: sr-only (screen reader only, visually hidden)
- On focus: show it (remove sr-only effects)

We need to override the sr-only styles on focus. A common approach:
```
className="absolute left-4 top-4 -translate-y-full focus:translate-y-0 focus:z-50 ..."
```
Or use a custom class. Let me check - the globals.css has .sr-only. So we need when focused to "un-apply" those styles. We could use:
`focus:static focus:w-auto focus:h-auto focus:p-4 focus:m-0 focus:overflow-visible focus:clip-auto`

Actually clip doesn't have "auto" in older CSS. Let me use a simpler approach - just make it always there but transparent/offscreen, and on focus move it into view. Or use the simpler `focus-within` technique.

Actually the simplest is to keep it as-is - the user might need to add custom CSS. In Tailwind, `focus:not-sr-only` doesn't exist. Let me change to a working approach:

<think>
For per-page metadata in Next.js App Router - pages that use "use client" cannot export metadata directly (metadata must be in server components). So for client components, we have two options:
1. Create a separate layout.tsx for each route that exports metadata
2. Use next/head (deprecated in App Router) or a custom Head component
3. Keep the page as server component and only wrap client parts

Actually in Next.js 14 App Router, if a page is a client component ("use client"), we can't export metadata from it. We need to either:
- Make the page a server component and import client components where needed
- Or create a layout for each route segment that has the metadata

Let me create layout files for the main sections to add metadata. Or we could use generateMetadata in a layout - but layout.tsx is already the root. We could add:
- app/products/layout.tsx - metadata for products
- app/contact/layout.tsx - metadata for contact
- etc.

Or simpler: create a metadata.ts or constants and have each page's parent layout export it. For nested routes like /products/online, the products layout would apply.

  contents: # 知己网站 MVP

> 移动端优先 · PC 共享布局 · 二级页面全可点击 · SEO 与可访问性完善

## 页面结构

| 路径 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|
| `/` | 首页：品牌、目标市场、快捷入口 |
| `/products` | 产品矩阵：训练营、咨询、沙龙 |
| `/products/online` | 线上训练营 |
| `/products/consult` | 一对一高客单咨询 |
| `/products/salon` | 线下沙龙 |
| `/market/gaoxiao` | 高校职业力 |
| `/market/jiating` | 家庭幸福力 |
| `/market/zhichang` | 职场领导力 |
| `/market/liuliang` | 流量/内容 |
| `/cooperation` | 合作入口：企业、导师、流程 |
| `/contact` | 联系我们：表单、邮件、电话、飞书 |
| `/about` | 关于知己：三条主线、成果、学员反馈 |
| `/team` | 核心团队与合作资源 |

## 启动

```bash
cd /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/知己/web
npm run dev   # 端口 3199
```

## 构建

```bash
npm run build
# 静态导出到 out/
```

## 特性

- **移动端优先**：触摸目标 ≥44px、底部导航、安全区域
- **PC 共享**：同一套内容，响应式布局
- **SEO**：每页独立 metadata、keywords、Open Graph、JSON-LD
- **可访问性**：跳过链接、aria-label、focus-visible、减少动画偏好
- **sitemap.xml**：`/public/sitemap.xml`
- **robots.txt**：`/public/robots.txt`

## 开发验证规则

开发一个阶段后，**先访问** http://localhost:3199 验证，有问题直接处理再继续。

  todos: [{"id":"1","content":"创建自动验证脚本：启动服务、打开网站、检查错误","status":"in_progress"},{"id":"2","content":"更新 .cursorrules 与 Skill：开发后自动执行验证","status":"pending"}]

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/知己/web/scripts/verify-website.js
  contents: #!/usr/bin/env node
/**
 * 知己网站自动验证脚本
 * 1. 检查/启动开发服务器
 * 2. 验证所有页面可访问
 * 3. 自动打开网站
 * 4. 输出验证报告（有错误则 exit 1，便于 AI 识别并修复）
 */

const http = require("http")
const { spawn } = require("child_process")
const path = require("path")

const PORT = 3199
const BASE = `http://localhost:${PORT}`

// 所有需验证的页面路径（与 next.config trailingSlash 一致）
const PAGES = [
  "/",
  "/products/",
  "/products/online/",
  "/products/consult/",
  "/products/salon/",
  "/market/gaoxiao/",
  "/market/jiating/",
  "/market/zhichang/",
  "/market/liuliang/",
  "/cooperation/",
  "/contact/",
  "/about/",
  "/team/",
]

// 错误关键词：页面内容包含这些则视为验证失败
const ERROR_KEYWORDS = [
  "Server Error",
  "Application error",
  "not find module",
  "Error:",
  "404",
  "500",
]

function fetchPage(url) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const req = http.get(url, { timeout: 10000 }, (res) => {
      let data = ""
      res.on("data", (chunk) => (data += chunk))
      res.on("end", () => resolve({ status: res.statusCode, body: data }))
    })
    req.on("error", reject)
    req.on("timeout", () => {
      req.destroy()
      reject(new Error("timeout"))
    })
  })
}

function checkForErrors(body) {
  const found = []
  for (const kw of ERROR_KEYWORDS) {
    if (body.includes(kw)) found.push(kw)
  }
  return found
}

async function isServerRunning() {
  try {
    const { status } = await fetchPage(BASE)
    return status === 200
  } catch {
    return false
  }
}

function startDevServer() {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const cwd = path.resolve(__dirname, "..")
    const child = spawn("npm", ["run", "dev"], {
      cwd,
      stdio: "pipe",
      detached: true,
    })
    child.unref()
    // 等待服务器就绪
    const check = setInterval(async () => {
      if (await isServerRunning()) {
        clearInterval(check)
        resolve()
      }
    }, 500)
    setTimeout(() => {
      clearInterval(check)
      resolve()
    }, 15000)
  })
}

function openBrowser() {
  const url = BASE
  const platform = process.platform
  const cmd = platform === "darwin" ? "open" : platform === "win32" ? "start" : "xdg-open"
  spawn(cmd, [url], { stdio: "ignore", detached: true }).unref()
}

async function main() {
  console.log("🔍 知己网站 · 自动验证\n")

  // 1. 检查/启动服务器
  if (!(await isServerRunning())) {
    console.log("⏳ 开发服务器未运行，正在启动...")
    await startDevServer()
    await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 3000))
  }

  if (!(await isServerRunning())) {
    console.error("❌ 无法连接开发服务器，请手动执行: npm run dev")
    process.exit(1)
  }
  console.log("✅ 开发服务器已就绪\n")

  // 2. 验证所有页面
  const results = []
  for (const p of PAGES) {
    const url = BASE + p.replace(/^\//, "")
    try {
      const { status, body } = await fetchPage(url)
      const errors = checkForErrors(body)
      const ok = status === 200 && errors.length === 0
      results.push({ path: p, status, errors, ok })
    } catch (e) {
      results.push({ path: p, status: 0, errors: [e.message], ok: false })
    }
  }

  // 3. 输出报告
  const failed = results.filter((r) => !r.ok)
  const passed = results.filter((r) => r.ok)

  console.log("📋 验证结果:\n")
  for (const r of results) {
    const icon = r.ok ? "✅" : "❌"
    const detail = r.ok ? `HTTP ${r.status}` : r.errors.join(", ") || `HTTP ${r.status}`
    console.log(`  ${icon} ${r.path.padEnd(25)} ${detail}`)
  }

  console.log("\n" + "─".repeat(50))
  console.log(`通过: ${passed.length}/${results.length}`)

  // 4. 打开浏览器
  console.log("\n🌐 正在打开浏览器...")
  openBrowser()

  // 5. 有错误则 exit 1
  if (failed.length > 0) {
    console.log("\n⚠️ 发现错误，请修复后重新验证")
    process.exit(1)
  }
  console.log("\n✅ 验证通过")
  process.exit(0)
}

main().catch((e) => {
  console.error(e)
  process.exit(1)
})

---

## 一、验证脚本 `scripts/verify-website.js`

| 步骤 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|
| 1 | 检查开发服务器是否运行，未运行则后台启动 |
| 2 | 请求 13 个页面，检查 HTTP 200 及错误关键词 |
| 3 | 自动打开浏览器访问 http://localhost:3199 |
| 4 | 输出验证报告，有错误则 exit 1 |

**错误关键词**：`Server Error`、`Application error`、`not find module`、`Cannot find module`

---

## 四、AI 工作流

1. 开发完成后执行 `npm run verify`
2. 若 exit 1：根据报告定位并修复问题，再执行 `npm run verify`
3. 若 exit 0：验证通过，可继续下一阶段
